var chf_timerID = null;
var chf_timerOn = false;
var chf_timecount = 300;

function chf_init(){
          if (document.layers) {
                        chf_layerRef="document.layers";
                        chf_styleSwitch="";
                        chf_visibleVar="show";
						chf_what ="ns4";

          }else if(document.all){

                        chf_styleSwitch=".style";

                        chf_layerRef="document.getElementByID";

			chf_what="none";

	function chf_showCountryPicker(obj, popup,evt){
		chf_globalDDN_Id = popup;
		if(popup!="chf_other_countries")
		{
		  chf_globalHoverState = obj.firstChild;
		  chf_globalHoverState.className+=" chf_current";
		}
		chf_hideAll(); 
		chf_showLayer(popup, obj);
		chf_stopTime();
		
		if((document.getElementById("chf_htl")) && (popup=="chf_hotel_DDN") && (chf_globalHoverState.className.indexOf("chf_htl_active")!=-1))
			document.getElementById(popup).style.left="-1px";
		else if((document.getElementById("chf_holidays")) && (popup=="chf_holidays_DDN") && (chf_globalHoverState.className.indexOf("chf_holidays_active")!=-1))
			document.getElementById(popup).style.left="-1px";
			
		chf_doSomething(evt);	
		}
	
		function chf_hideAll(){
				chf_hideLayer('chf_other_countries');
				chf_hideLayer('chf_hotel_DDN');
				chf_hideLayer('chf_holidays_DDN');
				chf_hideLayer('chf_CustomerSupport');
				chf_hideLayer('chf_car_DDN');
				}
				

 function chf_hideLayer(layerName){
            var chf_ndl;
        	if(chf_check){
        		if (chf_what =="none"){return;}
        		else if (chf_what == "moz"){
        			document.getElementById(layerName).style.visibility="hidden";
        			}
        		else{
                  eval(chf_layerRef+'["'+layerName+'"]'+chf_styleSwitch+'.visibility="hidden"');
				}
        
        	}
        	else {return;}
        }
		
        function chf_showLayer(layerName, obj){
            var chf_ndl;
        	if(chf_check){
        		if (chf_what =="none"){
        			return;
        			}
	        	if (chf_what == "moz"){
        			document.getElementById(layerName).style.visibility="visible";
        			}
        		else{
                  eval(chf_layerRef+'["'+layerName+'"]'+chf_styleSwitch+'.visibility="visible"');
		     } 
		 }
        	else {return;}
		}


function chf_startTime() {
if (chf_timerOn == false && chf_globalDDN_Id!=null && chf_globalDDN_Id!='undefined') {
if(chf_globalDDN_Id=="chf_other_countries")
{
	chf_timerID=setTimeout( "chf_hideAll()" , chf_timecount);
}
else
{
 chf_hideAll();
 chf_globalHoverState.className = chf_globalHoverState.className.replace("chf_current","");
}
chf_timerOn = true;
}} 

function chf_stopTime() {
if (chf_timerOn) {
clearTimeout(chf_timerID);
chf_timerID = null;
chf_timerOn = false;
}}

document.onclick=function()
{
	chf_countryDDN = document.getElementById("chf_other_countries");
	chf_htlDDN= document.getElementById("chf_hotel_DDN");
	chf_holidaysDDN = document.getElementById("chf_holidays_DDN");
	chf_csupportDDN = document.getElementById("chf_CustomerSupport");
	
	if(chf_countryDDN!=null && chf_htlDDN!=null && chf_holidaysDDN!=null && chf_csupportDDN!=null)
	{
		if(chf_countryDDN.style.visibility=="visible" || chf_htlDDN.style.visibility=="visible" || chf_holidaysDDN.style.visibility == "visible" || chf_csupportDDN.style.visibility=="visible")
		{
			document.getElementById("chf_other_countries").style.visibility="hidden";
			document.getElementById("chf_hotel_DDN").style.visibility="hidden";
			document.getElementById("chf_holidays_DDN").style.visibility="hidden";
			document.getElementById("chf_CustomerSupport").style.visibility="hidden";
		}
	}
}

function chf_doSomething(e)
{
	if (!e) var e = window.event;
	e.cancelBubble = true;
	if (e.stopPropagation) e.stopPropagation();
}

<script>
var userInfo=null;
var ajxRequest=null;
var signStatus=null;
var searchKeyJSVal = '2878b7c0799|8006|465c|c6d2|b6cd27b'; 
try {
	ajxRequest = new window.XMLHttpRequest();
	if(ajxRequest.overrideMimeType) {
 	}
} catch(e) {
	ajxRequest = new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");
}
function chf_showLogin(chf_obj){
	chf_showLogin_1(chf_obj,true);
}

function chf_showLogin_1(chf_obj,mode) {
	if("chf_signin"!=chf_obj.parentNode.id){
		  signOutWork_1(mode);
	  }
	  return false;
}
function signOutWork(){
	signOutWork_1(true);
}
function signOutWork_1(mode){		
	document.getElementById("chf_register").style["display"]="block";
	document.getElementById("chf_signin").style["display"]="block";
    document.getElementById("chf_welcomeTxt").style["display"]="none";
    document.getElementById("chf_signout").style["display"]="none";
	document.getElementById("chf_mybookings").style["display"]="none";
	
	if(document.getElementById("mmtGuestCase") != null){
		document.getElementById("mmtGuestCase").style["display"]="none";
	}
	
	
	if(mode){
		try{signout();}catch(e){}
	}
	
	if(document.getElementById("mmtLoggedInCase")!=null){
		commonLogOut();
	}
	try{	
		mmt.social.services.fb.logout();		
	}catch(e){
		(new Image()).src = '/makemytrip/imagez/spacer.GiF?page=FBSignOut&clicked=signOutWork&searchKey='+searchKeyJSVal+'&errorName='+e.name+'&errorMsg='+e.message+'&errorNum='+(e.number & 0xffff)+'&errorDesc='+e.description;
	}		
	ajxRequest.open("POST","signout.do", true);
	ajxRequest.onreadystatechange=handleSignOutResponse;
	ajxRequest.send(null);
	
	if(mtrRewardStatusFromCookie!=undefined && mtrRewardStatusFromCookie!=""){
		if(isTravellerOnReviewCoco2=='true' && mtrAmount > 0 && isMTRPointsCalculator == true && mtrRewardStatusFromCookie=="on"){
			$("#mtrCocoDiv").html('');
			mtrAmount = 0;
			calcTotalAmount();
			disableService('MTR');
			obj.renderFareSummary(reviewFlights);
			showFeedback("MyTripReward discount removed",'hdrReviewDetail');
			
		}
	}
}

function handleSignOutResponse(){
	if(ajxRequest.readyState==4) {
		var response = ajxRequest.responseText;
		signStatus="signout";
	}
}

function regUser(){
	document.getElementById("chf_register").style["display"]="none";
	document.getElementById("chf_signin").style["display"]="none";
    document.getElementById("chf_welcomeTxt").style["display"]="block";
    document.getElementById("chf_signout").style["display"]="block";
	document.getElementById("chf_mybookings").style["display"]="block";
}
var userNameHeader = 'Guest';
document.getElementById("chf_welcomeTxt").innerHTML = "Welcome "+userNameHeader;
